<UserId.>101411309051629028007< /UserId.>< rate>
5<//rate>
< Text>
Chris and Ting are some of the best owners I've had the pleasure of talking with. They truly want their patrons to enjoy food, and boy will you! Pre-Covid, it was nice to be able to sit inside and see where the food comes from, unlike most larger restaurants.

Small spot tucked away in a shopping center, off of Santo Rd almost unnoticed right next to a laundromat.

Portions are ample enough to satisfy your appetite and you'll be wowed by the taste. Food and location feel like you're having food from your mom... if she made Thai. The Drunken Noodles, are amazing and the Pumpkin Curry is a must! Just ask Chris or Ting what they like and I'm sure they will steer you in the right direction.

Currently, everything is only for take out/delivery due to current conditions. I highly recommend calling your order in and picking it up to help support our local businesses and to meet the people here. Ordering from delivery services robs these places of needed income, and right now everyone can use the help.

I truly recommend this place if you're looking for good homemade style Thai food from a place that's just around the corner.</Text>

<Text>My daughter was saying she wanted Pho and that she and her friends went to a place on Ocean.  I found this place on google maps, but when we go here, she said this wasn't the place she went with her friends.  It was already pretty late so we got a table, at first it was less than half full.  They bring tea right away.  We ordered our food, my daughter got Pho, but I got the duck and bamboo noodle soup.  She said the Pho was ok and it smelled really good (actually when you walk in you smell the Pho broth).  The bamboo in my soup isn't your typical slice you get out of a can that many Chinese restaurants server.  I think they needed to cook the bamboo a little more, some was very chewy.  They serve a vinegar ginger sauce for the duck (they serve the duck with bones so watch out).  I wish the broth was a bit richer.

Overall the place is solid, service isn't too great, you order, you get your food, then you flag them down for the check.  My daughter never got her glass of water she request and she gave up and just drank tea instead.

About 8:30pm the place filled up quickly.  When we walked to our car, there was many people double parking, waiting for spaces.

I'll be back to try their other dish, but I'll increase my star points then.</Text><Pictures>None<//Pictures>< response>
None</response>

<userid>114662549215996420847</userid><user_name>Miriam Leon<//user_name><time>1607570828256<//time><rating>5<//rating>< text>
The carne asada tacos and the nachos are quite tasty but the horchata water is much too sweet. The staff is also very friendly and helpful but I don't like the fact that every time you buy a big order of nachos they give you a different price and they serve you only half of the container. When I reviewed this restaurant three years ago they used to serve you the full container in spite of the fact that they always gave you a different price when you ordered them. Nowadays if you want them to give you the whole container you have to buy the small one. Back then it didn't matter whether you bought the big container or the small one because they always gave you the correct amount of food. But I cannot deny the fact that I would love to tast the super burrito and the flan. I hope that I can do that very soon.<//text>
